From Cosy Doubles to Feature Doubles, we have a variety of bedrooms for you to choose from. All rooms are quirky and have their own individual charm.Please note due to the age of the building we do not have a lift. Book your stay Feature Double RoomOur Feature Double Bedrooms are incredibly spacious and comfortable. Fitted with a luxurious double bed to make sure you get a great night’s sleep. These bedrooms have a seating area, a perfect place for you to relax.Not pet friendly Book Executive Double RoomOur Executive Double Bedrooms are spacious and quirky with everything you would expect from an Old Coaching Inn. Some of these bedrooms due to location have an ornate bathtub, however they may not all have a shower.Not pet friendly Book Classic Double RoomA traditional unique room with comfortable double bed in the main building or first floor courtyard.Ideal for your overnight stay in Arundel and everything you need for a refreshing night’s sleep.Not pet friendly Book Courtyard Double/Twin RoomOur Courtyard Bedrooms are comfortable with everything you would expect from your stay. On the ground floor you can choose either a Super King Size Double Bed or a Twin-Bedded room, whilst on the 1st floor all bedrooms are Standard Double Beds.Be sure to let the Team know your preference when booking.Three of these bedrooms are pet friendly, please speak to the Team for more information.Ground floor rooms are not wheelchair friendly. Book Cosy Double RoomThese lovely cosy bedrooms are full of historical charm. Many years ago, these were the servants’ quarters and as a result they have a lower ceiling height. Some of them have been refurbished to a high standard in 2018. Some of these bedrooms boast some of the best views in the Hotel.Due to the lower ceiling height and in keeping with the historical nature these rooms have an ornate bathtub but no shower.Please note, these bedrooms are located on the hotels third floor and we do not have a lift although we offer plenty of spots to sit and rest.Not pet friendly Book Single RoomTravelling on your own? Why not check in to one of our small but very welcoming Single Bedrooms.Some of our single bedrooms have a view overlooking Arundel High Street.Not pet friendly Book Family SuiteWe are delighted to add a family Suite to our collection of quirky and comfortable rooms.Located on the 3rd floor of the hotel, the main bedroom has a four-poster bed, small seating area to sit and relax, new bathroom with bath and shower over. This room overlooks the charming High Street of Arundel, the second bedroom has a super king bed, and all the facilities of our other bedrooms. To stop the queue for the shower in the morning it even has its own shower in the room. (but no toilet)Please remember that the hotel does not have a lift, but we can assist with luggage to and from the room.Not pet friendlyThis Suite cannot be booked online so for further details, or to make a booking for the Suite please call 01903 882101 or email [email protected]. Accessible RoomConveniently located on the ground floor, our Accessible Room is thoughtfully designed to cater to the needs of guests with mobility challenges,This room offers spacious layouts, wheelchair-friendly access, and adapted bathrooms with grab rails and walk-in showers.         "text_clean": "Select Page\nA family friendly pub\nAt the heart of Arundel’s Town Square awaits The Red Lion. It’s doors opened over 300 years ago. On entering one is greeted warmly by a sea of : locals; visitors to the area; and highly attentive staff – but not necessarily in that order. Often you will find Chris the owner, if you are really fortunate his partner Samantha, they will ensure your visit is as pleasant as possible.\nQuench your thirst with an excellent beer or cider on tap, discover fine wines, sip boutique gins or premier spirits, perhaps explore some interesting guest ales from one of the many craft breweries in the area. At Christmas try our warm spiced wine or a flagon of our renowned hot cider with a dash of rum – it’s sure to thaw out the iciest of winter dragons. We also have tea and coffee and a range of alcohol free beverages.\nWe are dog friendly, we invite family groups and tables of friends or work colleagues to meet up. There are quiet corners for those who wish to enjoy a quiet drink or snack while surfing the web via our free wifi.\nFood is served every day\nOur menus include fresh Sussex produce with breakfasts on Saturday mornings (10am til Noon) and roasts on a Sunday. Try our Moules Marinière it is exceptional, sample our desserts they are mouth wateringly delicious.\nSunny beer garden\nEnjoy the large sunny beer garden with plenty of seating. There is a heated gazebo for the cooler evenings.\nLive music\nWe are open till midnight on Friday and Saturday nights featuring live bands or acoustic acts. There is an open mic night on the first Thursday of the month and the critically acclaimed Jailhouse Blues Club on the 3rd Thursday of the month. Stay up to date with our newsletter ‘The Rub’  with all the line-ups published early each month and emailed direct to subscribers.\nArthaus\nHow would you like to display your art in The Red Lion? We support artists and can feature work on our walls and our website.         "page_type": "home",
        "text_clean": "Open Navigation\nClose Navigation\nRecipe\n23 February 2021\nRoasted Butternut Squash Soup With Granola\n(Serves 4 – 5 people)\nSOUP INGREDIENTS\n30g Unsalted butter\n1tsp Olive oil\n100g Onion\n50g Fennel\n15g Celery\n1/2pc Garlic clove\n1pc Star aniseed\n1pc Butternut squash\n1pc Thyme sprig\n1/2pc Bay leaf\n500ml Chicken stock\n600ml Whole milk\nSalt, pepper and freshly grated nutmeg\nMETHOD\n1. Cut the squash length ways. Using a spoon, scoop out the seeds. Brush with oil and season with salt and pepper.\n2. Roast in oven at 350ºF until golden and soft.\n3. Cut the vegetables into a rough chop. Approx 1cm dice.\n4. Sweat the chopped vegetables, aniseed and garlic together.\n5. Add the chicken stock and milk, bring to the boil and simmer.\n6. Once cool enough to handle, scoop the roasted flesh from the squash. Add to the soup base and simmer for a further 15-20 minutes.\n7. Remove from the heat and blend until smooth.\n8. Using a ladle, pour and push the blended soup through a fine strainer.\n9. If required add more milk to correct the consistency.\n10. Taste and correct the seasoning with salt pepper and a little freshly grated nutmeg.\n11. Serve the soup in a warm bowl, top with a drizzle of crème fraiche and granola (see recipe).\nGRANOLA INGREDIENTS\n50g Large rolled oats\n25g Slithered almonds\n15g Pumpkin seeds\n15g Sunflower seeds\n5g Demerara sugar\n1 pinch Cinnamon, ground\n1/2 tsp Fennel seed\n1 pinch Salt, Maldon\n1 tbsp Apple purée\n1 tsp Clear honey\n1 tsp Oil: pumpkin seed or walnut\nMETHOD\n1. Warm the honey, apple purée and oil together with the cinnamon, ginger and salt.\n2. Place all of the dry ingredients into a large bowl. Add the warm apple purée and mix well.\n3. Place the mix evenly onto a sheet pan lined with parchment paper.\n4. Bake at 250°F for 45 min to an hour until golden in colour.\n5. Allow to cool.\n6. Break up and store in a sealed container for up to a week\nBack to Journal",
